paymentDateAdjustment) {\n   142→\n   143→    ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n   144→    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n   145→\n   146→    // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n   147→    // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n   148→    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n   149→    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n   150→    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxVanillaOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n
